CREATE TABLE subjectMatter
(
    EPISODE	VARCHAR(512),
    TITLE	VARCHAR(512),
    APPLE_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    AURORA_BOREALIS	VARCHAR(512),
    BARN	VARCHAR(512),
    BEACH	VARCHAR(512),
    BOAT	VARCHAR(512),
    BRIDGE	VARCHAR(512),
    BUILDING	VARCHAR(512),
    BUSHES	VARCHAR(512),
    CABIN	VARCHAR(512),
    CACTUS	VARCHAR(512),
    CIRCLE_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    CIRRUS	VARCHAR(512),
    CLIFF	VARCHAR(512),
    CLOUDS	VARCHAR(512),
    CONIFER	VARCHAR(512),
    CUMULUS	VARCHAR(512),
    DECIDUOUS	VARCHAR(512),
    DIANE_ANDRE	VARCHAR(512),
    DOCK	VARCHAR(512),
    DOUBLE_OVAL_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    FARM	VARCHAR(512),
    FENCE	VARCHAR(512),
    FIRE	VARCHAR(512),
    FLORIDA_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    FLOWERS	VARCHAR(512),
    FOG	VARCHAR(512),
    FRAMED	VARCHAR(512),
    GRASS	VARCHAR(512),
    GUEST	VARCHAR(512),
    HALF_CIRCLE_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    HALF_OVAL_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    HILLS	VARCHAR(512),
    LAKE	VARCHAR(512),
    LAKES	VARCHAR(512),
    LIGHTHOUSE	VARCHAR(512),
    MILL	VARCHAR(512),
    MOON	VARCHAR(512),
    MOUNTAIN	VARCHAR(512),
    MOUNTAINS	VARCHAR(512),
    NIGHT	VARCHAR(512),
    OCEAN	VARCHAR(512),
    OVAL_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    PALM_TREES	VARCHAR(512),
    PATH	VARCHAR(512),
    PERSON	VARCHAR(512),
    PORTRAIT	VARCHAR(512),
    RECTANGLE_3D_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    RECTANGULAR_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    RIVER	VARCHAR(512),
    ROCKS	VARCHAR(512),
    SEASHELL_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    SNOW	VARCHAR(512),
    SNOWY_MOUNTAIN	VARCHAR(512),
    SPLIT_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    STEVE_ROSS	VARCHAR(512),
    STRUCTURE	VARCHAR(512),
    SUN	VARCHAR(512),
    TOMB_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    TREE	VARCHAR(512),
    TREES	VARCHAR(512),
    TRIPLE_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    WATERFALL	VARCHAR(512),
    WAVES	VARCHAR(512),
    WINDMILL	VARCHAR(512),
    WINDOW_FRAME	VARCHAR(512),
    WINTER	VARCHAR(512),
    WOOD_FRAMED	VARCHAR(512)
);
